———————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————
                                 MARIO & LUIGI: 
                                PARTNERS IN TIME
                                 Text dumped by
                                  Kin_Tamashii
                                   Cleanup by
                                   Seándwalsh
                             Updated July 4th, 2021
———————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————
Note: This text dump is extracted from the North American version of the game, 
released November 28, 2005 for the Nintendo DS.

What follows is a cleaned-up presentation of all the text in the entire game--
not only dialogue but also menu text, item and monster lists, etc. At some 
points, it was necessary to take minor liberties with the spacing and 
formatting of the text's presentation. Text was extracted using a tool made by 
Kin_Tamashii, so this wouldn't have been possible without their help. Please 
check out their YouTube Channel: youtube.com/channel/UCU17GiQFxEy9tpmqAnn1jWg

There is a "raw" version of this text dump--showing all the extra bits of 
control code in the text, However, all such codes have been removed from 
this version to give it a cleaner presentation. Three separate text files
have been combined into one here before they were cleaned up by me. For 
more of my stuff check out the Marioverse Discord Server, the home of
Mario Lore discussion: https://discord.gg/eq7HVQQ 

This is the order in which the text is found in each file, and thus the 
order it will be presented in this document. The files have been placed
in the following order:

File: 'FEvData'
File: 'BMes'
File: 'mfset'

The following is a key for non-text representations in this document:
{A} = A Button
{B} = B Button
{X} = X Button
{Y} = Y Button
{R} = R Button
{+} = D-Pad
{S} = START Button
{#} = Variable (numerical)

For any questions, or if there are any errors, omissions, inconsistencies, or 
other issues, please contact me via the Marioverse Discord Server, at this
link: https://discord.gg/eq7HVQQ 

The format of this file is inspired by Rew's Compendium of Text Dumps, which 
covers Super Mario RPG: Legend of the Seven Stars and the first four Paper
Mario games. It is a very helpful resource.
